### Round 6: Detroit Grand Prix
*Date: 1985-06-23*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 16: Australian Grand Prix
*Date: 1985-11-03*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
